03167:   RequestOptions _setStreamType<T>(RequestOptions requestOptions) {
03168:     if (T != dynamic &&
03169:         !(requestOptions.responseType == ResponseType.bytes ||
03170:             requestOptions.responseType == ResponseType.stream)) {
03171:       if (T == String) {
03172:         requestOptions.responseType = ResponseType.plain;
03173:       } else {
03174:         requestOptions.responseType = ResponseType.json;
03175:       }
03176:     }
03177:     return requestOptions;
03178:   }
03179: 
03180:   String _combineBaseUrls(String dioBaseUrl, String? baseUrl) {
03181:     if (baseUrl == null || baseUrl.trim().isEmpty) {
03182:       return dioBaseUrl;
03183:     }
03184: 
03185:     final url = Uri.parse(baseUrl);
03186: 
03187:     if (url.isAbsolute) {
03188:       return url.toString();
03189:     }
03190: 
03191:     return Uri.parse(dioBaseUrl).resolveUri(url).toString();
03192:   }
03193: }

00058:               extensions: [
00059:                 TagExtension(
00060:                   tagsToExtend: {"img"},

00199:   Future<void> sendEmail(BuildContext context) async {
00200:     FocusScope.of(context).unfocus();
00201: 
00202:     if (maSinhVien.value.trim().isEmpty) {
00203:       showMailGuide(
00204:         context,
00205:         title: 'Thiếu mã sinh viên',
00206:         message:
00207:         'Chưa tìm thấy mã sinh viên trong cache. Vui lòng bổ sung mã sinh viên trong nội dung email trước khi gửi.',
00208:       );
00209:       return;
00210:     }
00211: 
00212:     isSending.value = true;
00213: 
00214:     try {
00215:       final attachmentPaths = images.map((x) => x.path).toList();
00216: 
00217:       final raw = await gmailChannel.invokeMethod('composeEmail', {
00218:         'to': recipientEmail,
00219:         'recipients': [recipientEmail],
00220:         'subject': subjectController.text.trim(),
00221:         'body': bodyController.text.trim(),
00222:         'attachmentPaths': attachmentPaths,
00223:         'attachments': attachmentPaths,
00224:         'preferGmail': true,
00225:       });
00226: 
00227:       final result = MailNativeResult.fromMap(raw);
00228: 
00229:       if (!context.mounted) return;
00230: 
00231:       if (result.success) {
00232:         showSuccess(
00233:           result.message.isNotEmpty
00234:               ? result.message
00235:               : 'Đã mở ứng dụng gửi email. Vui lòng kiểm tra nội dung và bấm Gửi.',
00236:         );
00237:       } else {
00238:         await copyManualContent();
00239: 
00240:         if (!context.mounted) return;
00241: 
00242:         showMailGuide(
00243:           context,
00244:           title: 'Không mở được ứng dụng gửi email',
00245:           message: result.message.isNotEmpty
00246:               ? '${result.message}\n\nNội dung email đã được copy.'
00247:               : 'Không thể mở ứng dụng gửi email. Nội dung email đã được copy.',
00248:         );
00249:       }
00250:     } on PlatformException catch (e) {
00251:       await copyManualContent();
00252: 
00253:       if (!context.mounted) return;
00254: 
00255:       showMailGuide(
00256:         context,
00257:         title: 'Không mở được ứng dụng gửi email',
00258:         message: '${e.message ?? e.code}\n\nNội dung email đã được copy.',
00259:       );
00260:     } catch (e) {
00261:       await copyManualContent();
00262: 
00263:       if (!context.mounted) return;
00264: 
00265:       showMailGuide(
00266:         context,
00267:         title: 'Không mở được ứng dụng gửi email',
00268:         message: 'Lỗi: $e\n\nNội dung email đã được copy.',
00269:       );
00270:     } finally {
00271:       isSending.value = false;
00272:     }
00273:   }

00054:       data: {
00055:         'username': username,
00056:         'password': password,

00446:   // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
00447:   // Mobile API xem điểm mới: /api/mobile/diem-sinh-vien/brc1|brc2|brc3
00448:   // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
00449: 
00450:   String _toMobileBrcKey(String kieuTruong) {
00451:     switch (kieuTruong) {
00452:       case 'BangKep':
00453:       case 'BRC2':
00454:       case 'brc2':
00455:         return 'brc2';
00456:       case 'TruongGui':
00457:       case 'BRC3':
00458:       case 'brc3':
00459:         return 'brc3';
00460:       case 'TruongChinh':
00461:       case 'BRC1':
00462:       case 'brc1':
00463:       default:
00464:         return 'brc1';
00465:     }
00466:   }
00467: 
00468:   Future<Map<String, dynamic>> getDiemSinhVienMobileFull(
00469:     String kieuTruong,
00470:     bool xemCaMonNgoaiCtdt,
00471:   ) async {
00472:     final brc = _toMobileBrcKey(kieuTruong);
00473: 
00474:     String path;
00475:     if (brc == 'brc1') {
00476:       path =
00477:           '/api/mobile/diem-sinh-vien/brc1/full?xemCaMonNgoaiCtdt=$xemCaMonNgoaiCtdt';
00478:     } else if (brc == 'brc2') {
00479:       path = '/api/mobile/diem-sinh-vien/brc2/full';
00480:     } else {
00481:       path =
00482:           '/api/mobile/diem-sinh-vien/brc3/full?xemCaMonNgoaiCtdt=$xemCaMonNgoaiCtdt&includeChungChi=true&includeMonThieuDiem=true';
00483:     }
00484: 
00485:     final response = await _dio.get<Map<String, dynamic>>(path);
00486:     return response.data ?? <String, dynamic>{};
00487:   }
00488: 
00489:   Future<List<Map<String, dynamic>>> getChungChiMobile(
00490:     String kieuTruong,
00491:   ) async {
00492:     final brc = _toMobileBrcKey(kieuTruong);
00493: 
00494:     if (brc == 'brc2') {
00495:       return <Map<String, dynamic>>[];
00496:     }
00497: 
00498:     final response = await _dio.get<List<dynamic>>(
00499:       '/api/mobile/diem-sinh-vien/$brc/chung-chi',
00500:     );
00501: 
00502:     return (response.data ?? [])
00503:         .whereType<Map>()
00504:         .map((e) => Map<String, dynamic>.from(e))
00505:         .toList();
00506:   }
00507: 
00508:   Future<List<DiemHocPhanModel>> getDiemHocPhanHocKyMobile(
00509:     String idHocKy,
00510:     String kieuTruong,
00511:     String idHocPhan,
00512:   ) async {
00513:     final brc = _toMobileBrcKey(kieuTruong);
00514: 
00515:     final response = await _dio.get<List<dynamic>>(
00516:       '/api/mobile/diem-sinh-vien/$brc/hoc-ky/$idHocKy/hoc-phan/$idHocPhan/diem-chi-tiet',
00517:     );
00518: 
00519:     return (response.data ?? []).whereType<Map>().map((e) {
00520:       final map = Map<String, dynamic>.from(e);
00521: 
00522:       return DiemHocPhanModel.fromJson({
00523:         ...map,
00524:         'loaiDiemHocPhan':
00525:             map['banChatKyThi'] ?? map['loaiDiemHocPhan'] ?? map['RES_NATURE'],
00526:         'trongSo': (map['trongSo'] ?? map['coeffi'] ?? map['COEFFI'])
00527:             ?.toString(),
00528:         'diemHe10': (map['diem'] ?? map['resPnt'] ?? map['RES_PNT'])
00529:             ?.toString(),
00530:       });
00531:     }).toList();

00090:   _checkBio() async {
00091:     String name = await DataRepository().getSecureSaveKey(kLoginUserName) ?? '';
00092:     if (name.isNotEmpty) {
00093:       _emailController.text = name;
00094:     }
00095: 
00096:     try {
00097:       isEnableLoginBio =
00098:           (await DataRepository().getSecureSaveKey(kLoginEnableBio) ?? '')
00099:               .isNotEmpty;
00100:     } catch (e) {}
00101: 
00102:     final List<BiometricType> availableBiometrics =
00103:         await auth.getAvailableBiometrics();
00104: 
00105:     if (availableBiometrics.isEmpty) {
00106:       // NO biometrics are enrolled.
00107:       isDeviceSupportBio = false;
00108:       return;
00109:     }
00110: 
00111:     if (availableBiometrics.contains(BiometricType.strong) ||
00112:         availableBiometrics.contains(BiometricType.face) ||
00113:         availableBiometrics.contains(BiometricType.fingerprint)) {
00114:       // Specific types of biometrics are available.
00115:       // Use checks like this with caution!
00116:       setState(() {
00117:         isDeviceSupportBio = true;
00118:         isBioByFaceId = availableBiometrics.contains(BiometricType.face);
00119:       });

00308:             if (state is AuthShowHub) {
00309:               Utils.showProgress(hubContext);
00310:             }
00311: 
00312:             if (state is AuthDismissHub) {
00313:               Utils.dismissProgress(hubContext);
00314:             }
00315:           },
00316:           child: BlocBuilder<AuthCubit, AuthState>(
00317:             bloc: _authCubit,
00318:             builder: (context, state) {
00319:               return Stack(
00320:                 children: [
00321:                   const _LoginBackground(),
00322: 
00323:                   SafeArea(
00324:                     child: LayoutBuilder(
00325:                       builder: (context, constraints) {
00326:                         final double screenWidth = constraints.maxWidth;
00327:                         final double screenHeight = constraints.maxHeight;
00328: 
00329:                         final double horizontalPadding =
00330:                         screenWidth < 390 ? 24 : 30;
00331: 
00332:                         // Chỉnh card đăng nhập lên/xuống ở đây.
00333:                         // Tăng số này nếu muốn div đăng nhập xuống thấp hơn.
00334:                         final double cardTop = screenHeight < 720
00335:                             ? 155
00336:                             : screenHeight < 800
00337:                             ? 175
00338:                             : 200;
00339: 
00340:                         return SingleChildScrollView(
00341:                           physics: const BouncingScrollPhysics(),
00342:                           padding: EdgeInsets.fromLTRB(
00343:                             horizontalPadding,
00344:                             cardTop,
00345:                             horizontalPadding,
00346:                             24,
00347:                           ),
00348:                           child: _LoginCard(
00349:                             studentCodeController: _studentCodeController,
00350:                             passwordController: _passwordController,
00351:                             obscurePassword: _obscurePassword,
00352:                             isDeviceSupportBio: isDeviceSupportBio,
00353:                             isBioByFaceId: isBioByFaceId,
00354:                             onLogin: _login,
00355:                             onBioLogin: _loginWithBio,
00356:                             onTogglePassword: () {
00357:                               setState(() {
00358:                                 _obscurePassword = !_obscurePassword;
00359:                               });
00360:                             },
00361:                           ),
00362:                         );
00363:                       },
00364:                     ),
00365:                   ),
00366:                 ],
00367:               );
00368:             },
00369:           ),
00370:         ),
00371:       ),
00372:     );
00373:   }
00374: }

00502: class _InputField extends StatelessWidget {
00503:   const _InputField({
00504:     required this.controller,
00505:     required this.icon,
00506:     required this.hintText,
00507:     this.suffixIcon,
00508:     this.onSuffixTap,
00509:     this.obscureText = false,
00510:   });
00511: 
00512:   final TextEditingController controller;
00513:   final IconData icon;
00514:   final String hintText;
00515:   final IconData? suffixIcon;
00516:   final VoidCallback? onSuffixTap;
00517:   final bool obscureText;
00518: 
00519:   @override
00520:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
00521:     return _GlassLikeBox(
00522:       height: 56,
00523:       child: TextField(
00524:         controller: controller,
00525:         obscureText: obscureText,
00526:         style: const TextStyle(
00527:           color: _VCoreLoginScreenV3State.textDark,
00528:           fontSize: AppFontSizes.mediumLarge,
00529:           fontWeight: FontWeight.w500,
00530:         ),
00531:         decoration: InputDecoration(
00532:           border: InputBorder.none,
00533:           hintText: hintText,
00534:           hintStyle: const TextStyle(
00535:             color: _VCoreLoginScreenV3State.hint,
00536:             fontSize: AppFontSizes.mediumLarge,
00537:             fontWeight: FontWeight.w500,
00538:           ),
00539:           prefixIcon: Icon(
00540:             icon,
00541:             color: _VCoreLoginScreenV3State.green,
00542:             size: 24,
00543:           ),
00544:           suffixIcon: suffixIcon == null
00545:               ? null
00546:               : InkWell(
00547:             onTap: onSuffixTap,
00548:             borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(24),
00549:             child: Icon(
00550:               suffixIcon,
00551:               color: _VCoreLoginScreenV3State.textMuted,
00552:               size: 22,
00553:             ),
00554:           ),
00555:           contentPadding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(

00557:           ),
00558:         ),
00559:       ),
